## Dynamic Streams

`AEGP_DynamicStreamSuite` accesses and manipulates paint and text streams.

Use `AEGP_GetStreamGroupingType` and `AEGP_GetDynamicStreamFlags` to identify the stream before attempting to use functions which only work on certain stream types.

Also note that, often, you can simply use [Stream Suite](#stream-suite) calls to work with dynamic streams. On the other hand, only those functions specific to dynamic streams are in this suite.

### AEGP_DynamicStreamSuite4

| **Function**                      | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
|-----------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_GetNewStreamRefForLayer`    | Retrieves the AEGP_StreamRefH corresponding to the layer. This function is used to initiate a recursive walk of the layer's streams.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewStreamRefForLayer(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID    aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_LayerH      layerH,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  *streamPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| `AEGP_GetNewStreamRefForMask`     | Retrieves the AEGP_StreamRefH corresponding to the mask.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewStreamRefForMask(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID    aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH    maskH,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  *streamPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_GetStreamDepth`             | Retrieves the number of sub-streams associated with the given `AEGP_StreamRefH`.<br/>The initial layer has a depth of 0.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetStreamDepth(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_long           *depthPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_GetStreamGroupingType`      | Retrieves the grouping type for the given `AEGP_StreamRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetStreamGroupingType(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH          streamH,<br/>  AEGP_StreamGroupingType  *group_typeP);<br/>```<br/><br/>AEGP_StreamGroupingType will be one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_NONE`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_LEAF`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_NAMED_GROUP`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_INDEXED_GROUP`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_GetNumStreamsInGroup`       | Retrieves the number of streams associated with the given `AEGP_StreamRefH`.<br/>This function will return an error if called with an `AEGP_StreamRefH` with type `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_LEAF`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNumStreamsInGroup(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_long           *num_streamsPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_GetDynamicStreamFlags`      | Retrieves the flags for a given AEGP_StreamRefH.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetDynamicStreamFlags(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH      streamH,<br/>  AEGP_DynStreamFlags  *flagsP);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_DynStreamFlags` will be one of the following:<br/><br/>- `AEGP_DynStreamFlag_ACTIVE_EYEBALL` means that the stream is available for reading and writing.<br/>- `AEGP_DynStreamFlag_HIDDEN` means that, while the stream is still readable/writable, it may not currently be visible in the UI.<br/>- `AEGP_DynStreamFlag_DISABLED` A read-only flag. Indicates whether the `AEGP_StreamRefH` is grayed out in the UI.<br/>  Note that as of CS5, this flag will not be returned if a parameter is disabled.<br/>  Instead, check `PF_PUI_DISABLED` in [Parameter UI Flags](../effect-basics/PF_ParamDef.md#parameter-ui-flags).<br/>- `AEGP_DynStreamFlag_ELIDED` A read-only flag. Indicates that the `AEGP_StreamRefH` is read-only, the user never sees it.<br/>  However, the children are still seen and not indented in the Timeline panel.<br/>- `AEGP_DynStreamFlag_SHOWN_WHEN_EMPTY` New in CS6. A read-only flag. Indicates that this stream group should be shown when empty.<br/>- `AEGP_DynStreamFlag_SKIP_REVEAL_WHEN_UNHIDDEN` New in CS6. A read-only flag. Indicates that this stream property will not be automatically revealed when un-hidden. |
| `AEGP_SetDynamicStreamFlag`       | Sets the specified flag for the `AEGP_StreamRefH`.<br/><br/>Note: flags must be set individually. Undoable if `undoableB` is `TRUE`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetDynamicStreamFlag(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH      streamH,<br/>  AEGP_DynStreamFlags  one_flag,<br/>  A_Boolean            undoableB,<br/>  A_Boolean            setB);<br/>```<br/><br/>This call may be used to dynamically show or hide parameters, by setting and clearing `AEGP_DynStreamFlag_HIDDEN`.<br/>However, `AEGP_DynStreamFlag_DISABLED` may not be set.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_GetNewStreamRefByIndex`     | Retrieves a sub-stream by index from a given `AEGP_StreamRefH`. Cannot be used on streams of type `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_LEAF`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewStreamRefByIndex(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID    aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  parent_groupH,<br/>  A_long           indexL,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  *streamPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_GetNewStreamRefByMatchname` | Retrieves a sub-stream by match name from a given `AEGP_StreamRefH`. Only legal for `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_NAMED_GROUP`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewStreamRefByMatchname(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID    aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  parent_groupH,<br/>  const A_char     *match_nameZ,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  *streamPH);<br/>```<br/><br/>Here are some handy stream names, for which references may be retrieved:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_MASK_PARADE`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_MASK_ATOM`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamName_MASK_FEATHER`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamName_MASK_OPACITY`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamName_MASK_OFFSET`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_EFFECT_PARADE`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_LAYER`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_AV_LAYER`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_TEXT_LAYER`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_CAMERA_LAYER`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_LIGHT_LAYER`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_AUDIO`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_MATERIAL_OPTIONS`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_TRANSFORM`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_LIGHT_OPTIONS`<br/>> - `AEGP_StreamGroupName_CAMERA_OPTIONS`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| `AEGP_DeleteStream`               | Deletes the specified stream from a stream grouping.<br/>Note that the caller must still dispose of any `AEGP_StreamRefH` it's already acquired (allocated) via the API. Undoable.<br/>Only valid for children of type `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_INDEXED_GROUP`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DeleteStream(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH);<br/>```<br/><br/>Note: as of 6.5, if a stream is deleted while it or any child stream is selected, the current composition selection will become `NULL`.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_ReorderStream`              | Sets the new index of the specified `AEGP_StreamRefH`. Undoable.<br/>Only valid for children of `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_INDEXED_GROUP`.<br/>The `AEGP_StreamRefH` is updated to refer to the newly-ordered stream.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_ReorderStream(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH<br/>  A_long           new_indexL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_DuplicateStream`            | Duplicates the specified stream and appends it to the stream group.<br/>Undoable.<br/>Only valid for children of `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_INDEXED_GROUP`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DuplicateStream(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID    aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_long           *new_indexPL0);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_SetStreamName`              | Sets the name of the given `AEGP_StreamRefH`. Undoable. nameZ points to a null terminated UTF-16 string.<br/>Only valid for children of `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_INDEXED_GROUP`.<br/><br/>NOTE: If you retrieve the name with force_englishB set to `TRUE`, you will get the canonical, UNchanged name of the stream.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetStreamName(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH    streamH,<br/>  const A_UTF16Char  *nameZ);<br/>```<br/><br/>Note: Use this on an effect stream's group to change the display name of an effect.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_CanAddStream`               | Returns whether or not it is currently possible to add a stream through the API.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_CanAddStream(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  group_streamH,<br/>  const A_char     *match_nameZ,<br/>  A_Boolean        *can_addPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_AddStream`                  | Adds a stream to the specified stream group. Undoable. Only valid for `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_INDEXED_GROUP`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_AddStream(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID    aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  indxd_grp_streamH,<br/>  const A_char     *match_nameZ,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  *streamPH0);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| `AEGP_GetMatchName`               | Retrieves the match name for the specified `AEGP_StreamRefH`.<br/><br/>Note that this may differ from the display name, which can be retrieves using `AEGP_GetStreamName`, in [AEGP_StreamSuite5](#aegp_streamsuite5).<br/>`nameZ` can be up to `AEGP_MAX_STREAM_MATCH_NAME_SIZE` in length.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMatchName(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_char           *nameZ);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_GetNewParentStreamRef`      | Retrieves an `AEGP_StreamRefH` for the parent of the specified `AEGP_StreamRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewParentStreamRef(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID    plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  *parentPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_GetStreamIsModified`        | Returns whether or not the specified `AEGP_StreamRefH` has been modified.<br/><br/>Note: the same result is available throught the After Effect user interface by typing "UU" with the composition selected.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetStreamIsModified(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_Boolean        *modifiedPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| `AEGP_GetStreamIndexInParent`     | Retrieves the index of a given stream, relative to its parent stream.<br/>Only valid for children of `AEGP_StreamGroupingType_INDEXED_GROUP`<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetStreamIndexInParent(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_long           *indexPL);<br/>```<br/><br/>NOTE: As mentioned *elsewhere*, `AEGP_StreamRefHs` don't persist across function calls.<br/>If streams are re-ordered, added or removed, all `AEGP_StreamRefHs` previously retrieved may be invalidated.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_IsSeparationLeader`         | Valid on leaf streams only. Returns true if this stream is a multidimensional stream that can have its dimensions separated,<br/>though they may not be currently separated.<br/><br/>Terminology: A Leader is the stream that can be separated,<br/>a Follower is one of N automatic streams that correspond to the N dimensions of the Leader.<br/><br/>A Leader isn't always separated, call `AEGP_AreDimensionsSeparated` to find out if it is.<br/>As of CS4, the only stream that is ever separarated is the layer's Position property.<br/>Please *do not* write code assuming that, we anticipate allowing separation of more streams in the future.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_IsSeparationLeader(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_Boolean        *leaderPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| `AEGP_AreDimensionsSeparated`     | Methods such as `AEGP_GetNewKeyframeValue` that work on keyframe indices will<br/>most definitely *not* work on the Leader property, you will need to retrieve and operate on the Followers explicitly.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_AreDimensionsSeparated(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_Boolean        *separatedPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_SetDimensionsSeparated`     | Valid only if `AEGP_IsSeparationLeader()` is `true`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_AreDimensionsSeparated(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_Boolean        *separatedPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_GetSeparationFollower`      | Retrieve the Follower stream corresponding to a given dimension of the Leader stream.<br/>`dimS` can range from `0` to `AEGP_GetStreamValueDimensionality(lea der_streamH) - 1`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetSeparationFollower(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  leader_streamH<br/>  A_short          dimS,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  *follower_streamPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| `AEGP_IsSeparationFollower`       | Valid on leaf streams only.<br/>Returns `true` if this stream is a one dimensional property that represents one of the dimensions of a Leader.<br/>You can retrieve stream from the Leader using `AEGP_GetSeparationFollower()`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_IsSeparationFollower(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH<br/>  A_Boolean        *followerPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_GetSeparationLeader`        | Valid on separation Followers only, returns the Leader it is part of.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetSeparationLeader(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  follower_streamH,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  *leader_streamPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_GetSeparationDimension`     | Valid on separation Followers only, returns which dimension of the Leader it corresponds to.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetSeparationDimension(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  follower_streamH,<br/>  A_short          *dimPS);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |

---

## Working With Keyframes

Keyframes make After Effects what it is. AEGPs (andâ€¦ssshh, don't tell anyoneâ€¦effects) can use this suite to add, manipulate and remove keyframes from any keyframe-able stream.

### AEGP_KeyframeSuite3

| **Function**                           | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
|----------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_GetStreamNumKFs`                 | Retrieves the number of keyframes on the given stream.<br/>Returns `AEGP_NumKF_NO_DATA` if the stream is not keyframe-able.<br/>Also, note that a stream without keyframes isn't necessarily constant; it can be altered by expressions.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetStreamNumKFs(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_long           *num_kfsPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| `AEGP_GetKeyframeTime`                 | Retrieves the time of the specified keyframe.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetKeyframeTime(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH     streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex  index,<br/>  AEGP_LTimeMode      time_mode,<br/>  A_Time              *timePT);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_InsertKeyframe`                  | Adds a keyframe to the specified stream (at the specified composition or layer time).<br/>Returns the new keyframe's index.<br/>All indexes greater than the new index are now invalid (but you knew that).<br/>If there is already a keyframe at that time, the values will be updated.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_InsertKeyframe(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH     streamH,<br/>  AEGP_LTimeMode      time_mode,<br/>  const A_Time        *timePT,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex  *key_indexP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_DeleteKeyframe`                  | Deletes the specified keyframe.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DeleteKeyframe(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH     streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex  key_index);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_GetNewKeyframeValue`             | Creates and populates an `AEGP_StreamValue2` for the stream's value at the time of the keyframe.<br/>The returned `AEGP_StreamValue2` must be disposed of using `AEGP_DisposeStreamValue`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewKeyframeValue(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID       plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH     streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex  key_index,<br/>  AEGP_StreamValue2   *valueP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_SetKeyframeValue`                | Sets the stream's value at the time of the keyframe.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetKeyframeValue(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH          streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex       index,<br/>  const AEGP_StreamValue2  *valP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_GetStreamValueDimensionality`    | Retrieves the dimensionality of the stream's value.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetStreamValueDimensionality(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_short          *value_dimPS);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_GetStreamTemporalDimensionality` | Retrieves the temporal dimensionality of the stream.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetStreamTemporalDimensionality(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH  streamH,<br/>  A_short          *t_dimPS);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_GetNewKeyframeSpatialTangents`   | Returns the `AEGP_StreamValue2s` representing the stream's tangential values at the time of the keyframe.<br/><br/>The returned `AEGP_StreamValue2s` must be disposed of using `AEGP_DisposeStreamValue`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewKeyframeSpatialTangents(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID       plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH     streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex  key_index,<br/>  AEGP_StreamValue2   *in_tanP0,<br/>  AEGP_StreamValue2   *out_tanP0);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_SetKeyframeSpatialTangents`      | Specifies the tangential `AEGP_StreamValue2s` to be used for the stream's value at the time of the keyframe.<br/>The `AEGP_StreamValue2s` passed for in and out tangents are not adopted by After Effects, and must be disposed of using `AEGP_DisposeStreamValue`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetKeyframeSpatialTangents(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH          streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex       key_index,<br/>  const AEGP_StreamValue2  *in_tP0,<br/>  const AEGP_StreamValue2  *out_tP0);<br/>```<br/><br/>NOTE: In `AEGP_KeyframeSuite2` and prior versions, the values returned from this function<br/>were wrong when called on an effect point control stream or anchor point.<br/>They were not multiplied by the layer size. Now they are. |
| `AEGP_GetKeyframeTemporalEase`         | Retrieves the `AEGP_KeyframeEases` associated with the specified dimension of the stream's value at the time of the keyframe.<br/>`dimensionL` ranges from `0` to `(temporal_dimensionality -1)`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetKeyframeTemporalEase(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH     streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex  key_index,<br/>  A_long              dimensionL,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeEase   *in_easeP0,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeEase   *out_easeP0);<br/>```<br/><br/>NOTE: the returned ease values must be multiplied by layer height to match the values displayed in the After Effects UI.                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_SetKeyframeTemporalEase`         | Specifies the `AEGP_KeyframeEases` to be used for the stream's value at the time of the keyframe.<br/>`dimensionL` ranges from `0` to `(temporal_dimensionality -1)`.<br/>The `AEGP_KeyframeEases` passed are not adopted by After Effects.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetKeyframeTemporalEase(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH           streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex        key_index,<br/>  A_long                    dimL,<br/>  const AEGP_KeyframeEase   *in_P0,<br/>  const AEGP_KeyframeEase   *outP0);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_GetKeyframeFlags`                | Retrieves the flags currently set for the keyframe.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetKeyframeFlags(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH     streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex  key_index,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeFlags  *flagsP);<br/>```<br/><br/>`*flagsP` will be a combination of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_KeyframeFlag_NONE`<br/>> - `AEGP_KeyframeFlag_TEMPORAL_CONTINUOUS`<br/>> - `AEGP_KeyframeFlag_TEMPORAL_AUTOBEZIER`<br/>> - `AEGP_KeyframeFlag_SPATIAL_CONTINUOUS`<br/>> - `AEGP_KeyframeFlag_SPATIAL_AUTOBEZIER`<br/>> - `AEGP_KeyframeFlag_ROVING`                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_SetKeyframeFlag`                 | Sets the specified flag for the keyframe. Flags must be set individually.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetKeyframeFlag(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH     streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex  key_index,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeFlags  flag,<br/>  A_Boolean           valueB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_GetKeyframeInterpolation`        | Retrieves the in and out `AEGP_KeyframeInterpolationTypes` for the specified keyframe.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetKeyframeInterpolation(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH                 streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex              key_index,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeInterpolationType  *inP0,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeInterpolationType  *outP0);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_KeyframeInterpolationType` is one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_KeyInterp_NONE`<br/>> - `AEGP_KeyInterp_LINEAR`<br/>> - `AEGP_KeyInterp_BEZIER`<br/>> - `AEGP_KeyInterp_HOLD`                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_SetKeyframeInterpolation`        | Specifies the in and out `AEGP_KeyframeInterpolationTypes` to be used for the given keyframe.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetKeyframeInterpolation(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH                 streamH,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeIndex              key_index,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeInterpolationType  in_interp,<br/>  AEGP_KeyframeInterpolationType  out_interp);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_StartAddKeyframes`               | Informs After Effects that you're going to be adding several keyframes to the specified stream.<br/>After Effects will return an allocated opaque `AEGP_AddKeyframesInfoH`, for use with the calls below.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_StartAddKeyframes(<br/>  AEGP_StreamRefH         streamH,<br/>  AEGP_AddKeyframesInfoH  *akPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| `AEGP_AddKeyframes`                    | Adds a keyframe to the specified stream at the specified (layer or composition) time.<br/><br/>Note: this doesn't actually do anything to the stream's value.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_AddKeyframes(<br/>  AEGP_AddKeyframesInfoH  akH,<br/>  AEGP_LTimeMode          time_mode,<br/>  const A_Time            *timePT,<br/>  A_long                  *indexPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_SetAddKeyframe`                  | Sets the value of the specified keyframe.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetAddKeyframe(<br/>  AEGP_AddKeyframesInfoH   akH,<br/>  A_long                   indexL,<br/>  const AEGP_StreamValue2  *valueP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| `AEGP_EndAddKeyframes`                 | Tells After Effects you're done adding keyframes.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_EndAddKeyframes(<br/>  A_Boolean               addB,<br/>  AEGP_AddKeyframesInfoH  akH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |

---

## Adding Multiple Keyframes

Each time you call `AEGP_InsertKeyframe()`, the entire stream is added to the undo stack.

If you're adding one or two keyframes, this isn't a problem. However, if you're writing a keyframer, you'll want to do things the *right* way.

Before you begin adding keyframes, call the (very-appropriately-named) `AEGP_StartAddKeyframes`, passing it an opaque `AEGP_AddKeyframesInfoH`.

For each keyframe to add, call `AEGP_AddKeyframes` to set the time to be used (and get the newly-added keyframe's index), then `AEGP_SetAddKeyframe` to specify the value to be used.

Once you're finished, call `AEGP_EndAddKeyframes` to let know After Effects know it's time to add the changed parameter stream to the undo stack.

---

## Marker Streams

`AEGP_MarkerSuite` allows for direct manipulation of marker data.

### AEGP_MarkerSuite2

| **Function**                   | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
|--------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_NewMarker`               | Creates a new marker.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_NewMarker(<br/>  AEGP_MarkerValP  *markerPP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| `AEGP_DisposeMarker`           | Disposes of a marker.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DisposeMarker(<br/>  AEGP_MarkerValP  markerP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_DuplicateMarker`         | Duplicates a marker (didn't see *that* one coming, eh?).<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DuplicateMarker(<br/>  AEGP_MarkerValP  markerP,<br/>  AEGP_MarkerValP  *new_markerP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_SetMarkerFlag`           | Sets a marker flag's value.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMarkerFlag(<br/>  AEGP_MarkerValP      markerP,<br/>  AEGP_MarkerFlagType  flagType,<br/>  A_Boolean            valueB);<br/>```<br/><br/>Currently, AEGP_MarkerFlagType is one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_MarkerFlag_NONE`<br/>> - `AEGP_MarkerFlag_NAVIGATION`                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| `AEGP_GetMarkerFlag`           | Gets the value (see above) of a given `AEGP_MarkerFlagType`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMarkerFlag(<br/>  AEGP_ConstMarkerValP  markerP,<br/>  AEGP_MarkerFlagType   flagType<br/>  A_Boolean             *valueBP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| `AEGP_GetMarkerString`         | Retrieves the UTF-16, NULL-terminated string located in the specified marker field.<br/>Must be disposed of by caller using `AEGP_FreeMemHandle`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMarkerString(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID          id,<br/>  AEGP_ConstMarkerValP   markerP,<br/>  AEGP_MarkerStringType  strType,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle         *unicodePH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_SetMarkerString`         | Sets the specified field of a marker to the provided text.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMarkerString(<br/>  AEGP_MarkerValP        markerP,<br/>  AEGP_MarkerStringType  strType,<br/>  const A_u_short        *unicodeP,<br/>  A_long                 lengthL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_CountCuePointParams`     | Returns the number of cue point parameters.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_CountCuePointParams(<br/>  AEGP_ConstMarkerValP  markerP,<br/>  A_long                *paramsLP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_GetIndCuePointParam`     | Returns the cue point param at the specified index (which must be between `0` and `(cue point params -1)`.<br/>Returned handles are UTF-16, NULL-terminated strings, and must be disposed of by caller using `AEGP_FreeMemHandle`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetIndCuePointParam(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID         id,<br/>  AEGP_ConstMarkerValP  markerP,<br/>  A_long                param_indexL,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle        *unicodeKeyPH,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle        *uni_ValuePH);<br/>```                                      |
| `AEGP_SetIndCuePointParam`     | Set the value of an indexed cue point parameter to the specified value.<br/>`key_lengthL` is "number of unicode characters", and `value_lenL` is the length of the provided value.<br/>`unicode_KeyP` and `unicode_ValueP` point to UTF-16 data.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetIndCuePointParam(<br/>  AEGP_MarkerValP  markerP,<br/>  A_long           param_idxL,<br/>  const A_u_short  *unicode_KeyP,<br/>  A_long           key_lengthL,<br/>  const A_u_short  *unicode_ValueP,<br/>  A_long           value_lengthL);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_InsertCuePointParam`     | Inserts a cue point parameter.<br/>This call is following by `AEGP_SetIndCuePointParam` to actually set the data.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_InsertCuePointParam(<br/>  AEGP_MarkerValP  markerP,<br/>  A_long           param_idxL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_DeleteInd` CuePointParam | Deletes the cue point param at the specified index.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DeleteIndCuePointParam(<br/>  AEGP_MarkerValP  markerP,<br/>  A_long           param_idxL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_SetMarkerDuration`       | ```default<br/>AEGP_SetMarkerDuration(<br/>  AEGP_MarkerValP  markerP,<br/>  const A_Time     *durationPT);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_GetMarkerDuration`       | ```default<br/>AEGP_GetMarkerDuration(<br/>  AEGP_ConstMarkerValP  markerP,<br/>  A_Time                *durationPT);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |

## Mask Management

Access, manipulate, and delete a layer's masks.

### AEGP_MaskSuite6

| **Function**                  | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
|-------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_GetLayerNumMasks`       | Counts the masks applied to a layer,<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetLayerNumMasks(<br/>  AEGP_LayerH  aegp_layerH,<br/>  A_long       *num_masksPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_GetLayerMaskByIndex`    | Given a layer handle and mask index, returns a pointer to the mask handle.<br/>You must destroy the mask handle by using `AEGP_DisposeMask()`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetLayerMaskByIndex(<br/>  AEGP_LayerH    aegp_layerH,<br/>  A_long         mask_indexL,<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  *maskPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_DisposeMask`            | Dispose of a mask handle.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DisposeMask(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  maskH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_GetMaskInvert`          | Given a mask handle, determines if the mask is inverted or not.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMaskInvert(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  maskH,<br/>  A_Boolean      *invertPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_SetMaskInvert`          | Sets the inversion state of a mask.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMaskInvert(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  mask_refH,<br/>  A_Boolean      invertB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| `AEGP_GetMaskMode`            | Given a mask handle, returns the current mode of the mask.<br/><br/>`PF_MaskMode_NONE` does nothing,<br/>`PF_MaskMode_ADD` is the default behavior.<br/><br/>- `PF_MaskMode_NONE`<br/>- `PF_MaskMode_ADD`,<br/>- `PF_MaskMode_SUBTRACT`,<br/>- `PF_MaskMode_INTERSECT`,<br/>- `PF_MaskMode_LIGHTEN`,<br/>- `PF_MaskMode_DARKEN`,<br/>- `PF_MaskMode_DIFFERENCE`,<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMaskMode(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  maskH,<br/>  PF_MaskMode    *modeP);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_SetMaskMode`            | Sets the mode of the given mask.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMaskMode(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  maskH,<br/>  PF_MaskMode    mode);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_GetMaskMotionBlurState` | Retrieves the motion blur setting for the given mask.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMaskMotionBlurState(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH   mask_refH,<br/>  AEGP_MaskMBlur  *blur_stateP);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_MaskMBlur` will be one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_MaskMBlur_SAME_AS_LAYER`<br/>> - `AEGP_MaskMBlur_OFF`<br/>> - `AEGP_MaskMBlur_ON`                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_SetMaskMotionBlurState` | New in CS6. Sets the motion blur setting for the given mask.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMaskMotionBlurState(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH   mask_refH,<br/>  AEGP_MaskMBlur  blur_state);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_GetMaskFeatherFalloff`  | New in CS6. Gets the type of feather falloff for the given mask, either<br/>`AEGP_MaskFeatherFalloff_SMOOTH` or `AEGP_MaskFeatherFalloff_LINEAR`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMaskMotionBlurState(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH            mask_refH,<br/>  AEGP_MaskFeatherFalloff  *feather_falloffP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_SetMaskFeatherFalloff`  | Sets the type of feather falloff for the given mask.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMaskMotionBlurState(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH            mask_refH,<br/>  AEGP_MaskFeatherFalloff  feather_falloff);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| `AEGP_GetMaskName`            | Removed in CS4. Use `AEGP_GetNewStreamRefForMask` and the name functions in the Dynamic Stream Suite instead.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_SetMaskName`            |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_GetMaskID`              | Retrieves the `AEGP_MaskIDVal` for the given `AEGP_MaskRefH`, for use in uniquely identifying the mask.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMaskID(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH   mask_refH,<br/>  AEGP_MaskIDVal  *id_valP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_CreateNewMask`          | Creates a new mask on the referenced `AEGP_LayerH`, with zero nodes. | `AEGP_DeleteMaskFromLayer`    | ```default<br/>AEGP_DeleteMaskFromLayer(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  mask_refH);<br/>```<br/><br/>NOTE: As of 6.5, if you delete a mask and it or a child stream is selected, the current selection within the composition will become NULL.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_GetMaskColor`           | Retrieves the color of the specified mask.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMaskColor(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  mask_refH,<br/>  AEGP_ColorVal  *colorP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |

| `AEGP_GetMaskLockState`       | Retrieves the lock state of the specified mask.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMaskLockState(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  mask_refH,<br/>  A_Boolean      *is_lockedPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_SetMaskLockState`       | Sets the lock state of the specified mask.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMaskLockState(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  mask_refH,<br/>  A_Boolean      lockB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| `AEGP_GetMaskIsRotoBezier`    | Returns whether or not the given mask is used as a rotobezier.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMaskIsRotoBezier(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  mask_refH,<br/>  A_Boolean      *is_roto_bezierPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_SetMaskIsRotoBezier`    | Sets whether a given mask is to be used as a rotobezier.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMaskIsRotoBezier(<br/>  AEGP_MaskRefH  mask_refH,<br/>  A_Boolean      *is_roto_bezierPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_DuplicateMask`          | Duplicates a given `AEGP_MaskRefH`.
