## Mask Outlines

The Mask Suite above tells plug-ins about the masks on a layer, but not about the details of those masks.

This is because processing is required on After Effects' part to access the information; the information isn't just lying around.

Plug-ins access that information using this Mask Outline Suite.

### AEGP_MaskOutlineSuite3

| **Function**                     | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
|----------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_IsMaskOutlineOpen`         | Given an mask outline pointer (obtainable through the [Stream Suite](#stream-suite)),<br/>determines if the mask path is open or closed.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_IsMaskOutlineOpen(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineVal  *mask_outlineP,<br/>  A_Boolean            *openPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_SetMaskOutlineOpen`        | Sets the open state of the given mask outline.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMaskOutlineOpen(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineValH  mask_outlineH,<br/>  A_Boolean             openB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| `AEGP_GetMaskOutlineNumSegments` | Given a mask outline pointer, returns the number of segments in the path.<br/>`num_segmentsPL` is the total number of segments `[0...N-1]`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMaskOutlineNumSegments(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineVal  *mask_outlineP,<br/>  A_long               *num_segmentsPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_GetMaskOutlineVertexInfo`  | Given a mask outline pointer and a point between 0 and the total number of segments.<br/>For closed mask paths, `vertex[0]` is the same as `vertex[num_segments]`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMaskOutlineVertexInfo(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineVal  *mask_outlineP,<br/>  A_long               which_pointL,<br/>  AEGP_MaskVertex      *vertexP);<br/>```                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_SetMaskOutlineVertexInfo`  | Sets the vertex information for a given index.<br/>Setting vertex 0 is special; its in tangent will actually set the out tangent of the last vertex in the outline.<br/>Of course, `which_pointL` must be valid for the mask outline, or the function will return an error.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMaskOutlineVertexInfo(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineValH  mask_outlineH,<br/>  AEGP_VertexIndex      which_pointL,<br/>  AEGP_MaskVertex       *vertexP);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_CreateVertex`              | Creates a vertex at index position.<br/>All vertices which formerly had an `AEGP_VertexIndex` of position or greater will have their indices incremented by one.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_CreateVertex(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineValH  mask_outlineH,<br/>  AEGP_VertexIndex      position);.<br/>```<br/><br/>NOTE: All masks must have at least one vertex.                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_DeleteVertex`              | Removes a vertex from a mask.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DeleteVertex(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineValH  mask_outlineH,<br/>  AEGP_VertexIndex      index);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_GetMaskOutlineNumFeathers` | New in CS6.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DeleteVertex(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineValH  mask_outlineH,<br/>  A_long                *num_feathersPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_GetMaskOutlineFeatherInfo` | New in CS6.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMaskOutlineFeatherInfo(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineValH  mask_outlineH,<br/>  AEGP_FeatherIndex     which_featherL,<br/>  AEGP_MaskFeather      *featherP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_SetMaskOutlineFeatherInfo` | New in CS6. Feather must already exist; use `AEGP_CreateMaskOutlineFeather` first, if needed.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMaskOutlineFeatherInfo(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineValH    mask_outlineH,<br/>  AEGP_VertexIndex        which_featherL,<br/>  const AEGP_MaskFeather  *featherP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_CreateMaskOutlineFeather`  | New in CS6. Index of new feather is passed back in `insert_positionP`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_CreateMaskOutlineFeather(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineValH    mask_outlineH,<br/>  const AEGP_MaskFeather  *featherP0,<br/>  AEGP_FeatherIndex       *insert_positionP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_DeleteMaskOutlineFeather`  | New in CS6.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DeleteMaskOutlineFeather(<br/>  AEGP_MaskOutlineValH  mask_outlineH,<br/>  AEGP_FeatherIndex     index);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |

---

## Mask Feathering

New for CS6, masks can be feathered.

`AEGP_MaskFeather` is defined as follows:

```default
typedef struct {
  A_long                  segment;          // mask segment where feather is
  PF_FpLong               segment_sF;       // 0-1: feather location on segment
  PF_FpLong               radiusF;          // negative value allowed if type == AEGP_MaskFeatherType_INNER
  PF_FpShort              ui_corner_angleF; // 0-1: angle of UI handle on corners
  PF_FpShort              tensionF;         // 0-1: tension of boundary at feather pt
  AEGP_MaskFeatherInterp  interp;
  AEGP_MaskFeatherType    type;
} AEGP_MaskFeather;
```

`AEGP_MaskFeatherInterp` is either `AEGP_MaskFeatherInterp_NORMAL` or `AEGP_MaskFeatherInterp_HOLD_CW`.

`AEGP_MaskFeatherType` is either `AEGP_MaskFeatherType_OUTER` or `AEGP_MaskFeatherType_INNER`.

This suite enables AEGPs to get and set the text associated with text layers.

Note: to get started, retrieve an `AEGP_TextDocumentH` by calling `AEGP_GetLayerStreamValue`, above, and passing `AEGP_StreamType_TEXT_DOCUMENT` as the `AEGP_StreamType`.

---

## Working With Text Layers

This suite enables AEGPs to get and set the text associated with text layers.

<!-- note:

To get started, retrieve an ``AEGP_TextDocumentH`` by calling ``AEGP_GetLayerStreamValue`` above, and passing ``AEGP_StreamType_TEXT_DOCUMENT`` as the ``AEGP_StreamType``. -->

### AEGP_TextDocumentSuite1

| **Function**      | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
|-------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_GetNewText` | Retrieves the UTF-16, NULL-terminated string used in the `AEGP_TextDocumentH`.<br/><br/>Note: After Effects will allocate the `AEGP_MemHandle`;<br/>your plug-in must dispose of it when done using `AEGP_FreeMemHandle`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewText(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID       id,<br/>  AEGP_TextDocumentH  text_docH,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle      *unicodePH);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_SetText`    | Specifies the text to be used by the `AEGP_TextDocumentH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetText(<br/>  AEGP_TextDocumentH  text_docH,<br/>  const A_u_short     *unicodePS,<br/>  long                lengthL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                              |

## Working With Text Outlines

The `AEGP_TextLayerSuite` provides access to the actual outlines of the text used by text layers.

Once you have a path, you can manipulate it with [PF_PathQuerySuite1](../effect-details/working-with-paths.md#pf_pathquerysuite1) and [PF_PathDataSuite](../effect-details/working-with-paths.md#pf_pathdatasuite).

### AEGP_TextLayerSuite1

| **Function**                 | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_GetNewTextOutlines`    | Allocates and returns a handle to the `AEGP_TextOutlinesHs` associated with the specified layer.<br/>`outlinesPH` will be NULL if there are no `AEGP_TextOutlinesHs` associated with `layerH` (in other words, if it's not a text layer).<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewTextOutlines(<br/>  AEGP_LayerH         layerH,<br/>  const A_Time        *layer_timePT,<br/>  AEGP_TextOutlinesH  *outlinesPH);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_DisposeTextOutlines`   | Dispose of those outlines we allocated on your behalf!<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DisposeTextOutlines(<br/>  AEGP_TextOutlinesH  outlinesH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_GetNumTextOutlines`    | Retrieves the number of text outlines for the layer.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNumTextOutlines(<br/>  AEGP_TextOutlinesH  outlinesH,<br/>  A_long              *num_otlnsPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_GetIndexedTextOutline` | Returns a PF_PathOutlinePtr for the specifed text outline.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetIndexedTextOutline(<br/>  AEGP_TextOutlinesH  outlinesH,<br/>  A_long              path_indexL,<br/>  PF_PathOutlinePtr   *pathPP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                |

## Utility Functions

The Utility suite supplies error message handling, AEGP version checking and access to the undo stack.

Everything you need to keep After Effects and your plug-in tidy.

---

### AEGP_UtilitySuite6

| **Function**                         | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
|--------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_ReportInfo`                    | Displays dialog with name of the AEGP followed by the string passed.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_ReportInfo(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID  aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  const A_char   *info_stringZ);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| `AEGP_ReportInfoUnicode`             | New in CC. | `AEGP_GetDriverSpecVersion`          | Returns version of `AEGPDriver` plug-in (use to determine supported features).<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetDriverSpecVersion(<br/>  A_short  *major_versionPS,<br/>  A_short  *minor_versionPS);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_StartQuietErrors`              | Silences errors. Must be balanced with `AEGP_EndQuietErrors`.<br/>The `AEGP_ErrReportState` is an opaque structure private to After Effects.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_StartQuietErrors(<br/>  AEGP_ErrReportState  *err_stateP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_EndQuietErrors`                | Re-enables errors.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_EndQuietErrors(<br/>  AEGP_ErrReportState  *err_stateP)<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| `AEGP_StartUndoGroup`                | Add action(s) to the undo queue. The user may undo any actions between this and `AEGP_EndUndoGroup()`.<br/>The `undo_nameZ` will appear in the edit menu.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_StartUndoGroup(<br/>  const A_char  *undo_nameZ);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_EndUndoGroup`                  | Ends the undo list.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_EndUndoGroup();<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_RegisterWithAEGP`              | Returns an AEGP_PluginID, which effect plug-ins can then use in calls to many functions throughout the AEGP API.<br/>Effects should only call this function once, during `PF_Cmd_GLOBAL_SETUP`, and save the `AEGP_PluginID` for later use.<br/>The first parameter can be any value, and the second parameter should be the plug-in's match name.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_RegisterWithAEGP(<br/>  AEGP_GlobalRefcon  global_refcon,<br/>  const A_char       *plugin_nameZ,<br/>  AEGP_PluginID      *plugin_id);<br/>```                                                                                                                                 |
| `AEGP_GetMainHWND`                   | Retrieves After Effects' HWND; useful when displaying your own dialog on Windows.<br/>If you don't use After Effects' HWND, your modal dialog will not prevent interaction with the windows behind, and pain will ensue.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMainHWND(<br/>  void  *main_hwnd);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_ShowHideAllFloaters`           | Toggles whether or not floating palettes are displayed.<br/><br/>Use this with care; users get twitchy when you unexpectedly change the UI on them.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_ShowHideAllFloaters(<br/>  A_Boolean  include_tool_palB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_PaintPalGetForeColor`          | Retrieves the foreground color from the paint palette.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_PaintPalGetForeColor(<br/>  AEGP_ColorVal  *fore_colorP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_PaintPalGetBackColor`          | Retrieves the background color from the paint palette.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_PaintPalGetBackColor(<br/>  AEGP_ColorVal  *back_colorP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |

| `AEGP_ConvertHSFRatioToFpLong`       | Returns an `A_FpLong` interpretation of the given `A_Ratio`. Useful for horizontal scale factor interpretation.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_ConvertHSFRatioToFpLong(<br/>  A_Ratio    ratioR,<br/>  A_FpLong  *numberPF);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_CauseIdleRoutinesToBeCalled`   | This routine is safe to call from threads other than the main thread.<br/>It is asynchronous and will return before the idle handler is called.<br/><br/>The suite functions to get this function pointer are not thread safe; save it off in the main thread for use by the child thread.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_CauseIdleRoutinesToBeCalled(void);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_GetSuppressInteractiveUI`      | Returns whether After Effects is running without a user interface.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetSuppressInteractiveUI(<br/>  A_Boolean  *ui_is_suppressedPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_WriteToOSConsole`              | Sends a string to the OS console.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_WriteToOSConsole(<br/>  const A_char  *textZ);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_WriteToDebugLog`               | Writes a message to the debug log, or to the OS command line if After Effects was launched with the "-debug" option.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_WriteToDebugLog(<br/>  const A_char  *subsystemZ,<br/>  const A_char  *event_typeZ,<br/>  const A_char  *infoZ);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| `AEGP_GetLastErrorMessage`           | Retrieves the last error message displayed to the user, and its associated error number.<br/>Pass in the size of the character buffer to be returned.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetLastErrorMessage(<br/>  A_long  buffer_size,<br/>  A_char  *error_string,<br/>  A_Err   *error_num);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_IsScriptingAvailable`          | Returns `TRUE` if scripting is available to the plug-in.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_IsScriptingAvailable(<br/>  A_Boolean  *outAvailablePB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| `AEGP_ExecuteScript`                 | Have After Effects execute a script.<br/>The script passed in can be in either UTF-8 or the current application encoding (if platform_encodingB is passed in as TRUE).<br/><br/>The two out arguments are optional. The value of the last line of the script is what is passed back in outResultPH0.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_ExecuteScript(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID inPlugin_id,<br/>  const A_char *inScriptZ,<br/>  const A_Boolean platform_encodingB,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle *outResultPH0,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle *outErrStringPH0);<br/>```                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_HostIsActivated`               | Returns TRUE if the user has successfully activated After Effects.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_HostIsActivated(<br/>  A_Boolean  *is_activatedPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_GetPluginPlatformRef`          | On macOS, returns a `CFBundleRef` to your Mach-O plug-in, or NULL for a CFM plug-in.<br/>Always returns `NULL` on Windows (you can use an OS-specific entry point to capture your DLLInstance).<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetPluginPlatformRef(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID  plug_id,<br/>  void           **plat_refPPV);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_UpdateFontList`                | Rescans the system font list.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_UpdateFontList();<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_GetPluginPaths`                | New in CC. Returns a particular path associated with the plug-in:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_GetPathTypes_PLUGIN` - (Not Implemented) The path to the location of the plug-in itself.<br/>> - `AEGP_GetPathTypes_USER_PLUGIN` -The suite specific location of user specific plug-ins.<br/>> - `AEGP_GetPathTypes_ALLUSER_PLUGIN` - The suite specific location of plug-ins shared by all users.<br/>> - `AEGP_GetPathTypes_APP` - The After Effects .exe or .app location. Not plug-in specific.<br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetPluginPaths(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID      aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_GetPathTypes  path_type<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle     *unicode_pathPH);<br/>``` |

---

## Persistent Data Suite

Plug-ins have read and write access to persistent data in After Effects' preferences. AEGPs may add and manage their own persistent data using the following suite. The data entries are accessed by (section key, value key) pairs. It is recommended that plug-ins use their matchname as their section key, or as a prefix if using multiple section keys.

The available data types are `A_long`, `A_FpLong`, strings, and `void*`. `A_FpLongs` are stored with 6 decimal places of precision. There is no provision for specifying a different precision. String data supports the full 8-bit space. Only 0x00 is reserved for string ending. This makes them ideal for storing UTF-8 encoded strings, ISO 8859-1, and plain ASCII. Both section keys and value keys are of this type. For data types not represented by the simple data types provided, use data handles containing your custom data. void\* unstructured data allows you to store any kind of data. You must pass in a size in bytes along with the data.

When calling any of the functions to retrieve the value of a key, if a given key is not found, the default value is both written to the blob and returned as the value; if no default is provided, a blank value will be written and returned.

Note that this data is stored in the application's preferences, not in the project. As of 6.5, there is no way to store opaque AEGP-generated data in an After Effects project.

After Effects can handle plug-ins which change the preferences during their application; it checks the in-RAM copy of the prefs before acting upon pref-able settings, rather than relying on the saved prefs. It's like we *planned* this, or something!

### AEGP_PersistentDateSuite4

| **Function**                | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|-----------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_GetApplicationBlob`   | Obtains the handle to all persistent application data. Modifying this will modify the application.<br/><br/>The `AEGP_PersistentType` parameter is new in CC, and should be set to one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_PersistentType_MACHINE_SPECIFIC`,<br/>> - `AEGP_PersistentType_MACHINE_INDEPENDENT`,<br/>> - `AEGP_PersistentType_MACHINE_INDEPENDENT_RENDER`,<br/>> - `AEGP_PersistentType_MACHINE_INDEPENDENT_OUTPUT`,<br/>> - `AEGP_PersistentType_MACHINE_INDEPENDENT_COMPOSITION`<br/>> - `AEGP_PersistentType_MACHINE_SPECIFIC_TEXT`,<br/>> - `AEGP_PersistentType_MACHINE_SPECIFIC_PAINT`<br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetApplicationBlob(<br/>  AEGP_PersistentType   blob_type,<br/>  AEGP_PersistentBlobH  *blobPH);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_GetNumSections`       | Obtains the number of sections in the application blob.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNumSections(<br/>  AEGP_PersistentBlobH  blobH,<br/>  A_long                *num_sectionPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_GetSectionKeyByIndex` | Obtains the key at the given index.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetSectionKeyByIndex(<br/>  AEGP_PersistentBlobH  blobH,<br/>  A_long                section_index,<br/>  A_long                max_section_size,<br/>  A_char                *section_keyZ);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_DoesKeyExist`         | Returns whether or not a given key/value pair exists with the blob.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DoesKeyExist(<br/>  AEGP_PersistentBlobH  blobH,<br/>  const A_char          *section_keyZ,<br/>  const A_char          *value_keyZ,<br/>  A_Boolean             *existsPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_GetNumKeys`           | Retrieves the number of value keys in the section.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNumKeys(<br/>  AEGP_PersistentBlobH  blobH,<br/>  const A_char          *section_keyZ,<br/>  A_long                *num_keysPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_GetValueKeyByIndex`   | Retrieves the value of the indexed key.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetValueKeyByIndex(<br/>  AEGP_PersistentBlobH  blobH,<br/>  const A_char          *section_keyZ,<br/>  A_long                key_index,<br/>  A_long                max_key_size,<br/>  A_char                *value_keyZ);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |

!!! note
 For the functions below, if a given key is not found, the default value is both written to the blob and returned as the value;
if no default is provided, a blank value will be written and returned.

| **Function**             | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |

## Color Management

We've provided a function so AEGPs can obtain information on After Effects' current color management settings.

### AEGP_ColorSettingsSuite5

| **Function**                            | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
|-----------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_GetBlendingTables`                | Retrieves the current opaque `PF_EffectBlendingTables`, for use with `AEGP_TransferRect`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetBlendingTables(<br/>  PR_RenderContextH        render_contextH,<br/>  PF_EffectBlendingTables  *blending_tables);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_DoesViewHaveColorSpaceXform`      | Returns whether there is a colorspace transform applied to the current item view.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DoesViewHaveColorSpaceXform(<br/>  AEGP_ItemViewP  viewP,<br/>  A_Boolean       *has_xformPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_XformWorkingToViewColorSpace`     | Changes the view colorspace of the source to be the working colorspace of the destination.<br/>Source and destination can be the same.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_XformWorkingToViewColorSpace(<br/>  AEGP_ItemViewP  viewP,<br/>  AEGP_WorldH     srcH,<br/>  AEGP_WorldH     dstH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_GetNewWorkingSpaceColorProfile`   | Retrieves the opaque current working space ICC profile. Must be disposed.<br/>The "New" in the name does not indicate that you're making up a new profile; rather, it's part of our function naming standard;<br/>anything with "New" in the name allocates something which the caller must dispose.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewWorkingSpaceColorProfile(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID   aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle  *icc_profPH);<br/>```                                              |

| `AEGP_GetNewICCProfileFromColorProfile` | Retrieves a new ICC profile (stored in an `AEGP_MemHandle`) representing the specified color profile.<br/>Returned `AEGP_MemHandle` must be disposed by the caller.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewICCProfile FromColorProfile(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID            plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_ConstColorProfileP  profileP,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle           *profilePH);<br/>```                                                                                                                       |
| `AEGP_GetNewColorProfileDescription`    | Returns a textual description of the specified color profile.<br/>Text will be a null-terminated UTF16 string, which must be disposed by the caller.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewColorProfileDescription(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID            aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_ConstColorProfileP  profileP,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle           *unicode_descPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_DisposeColorProfile`              | Disposes of a color profile, obtained using other functions in this suite.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DisposeColorProfile(<br/>  AEGP_ColorProfileP  profileP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_GetColorProfileApproximateGamma`  | Returns a floating point number approximating the gamma setting used by the specified color profile.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetColorProfileApproximateGamma(<br/>  AEGP_ConstColorProfileP  profileP,<br/>  A_FpShort                *approx_gammaP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_IsRGBColorProfile`                | Returns whether the specified color profile is RGB.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_IsRGBColorProfile(<br/>  AEGP_ConstColorProfileP  profileP,<br/>  A_Boolean                *is_rgbPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_SetWorkingColorSpace`             | Sets the working space to the passed color profile.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetWorkingColorSpace(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID            aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_CompH               compH,<br/>  AEGP_ConstColorProfileP  color_profileP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_IsOCIOColorManagementUsed`        | Check if the current project is using the OCIO color engine or not.<br/>Returns true if current project uses OCIO color managed mode.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_IsOCIOColorManagementUsed(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID  aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  A_Boolean      *is_OCIOColorManagementUsedPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                  |

The returned strings must be disposed by the caller.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGPD_GetOCIODisplayColorSpace(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID   aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle  *ocio_displayH,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle  *ocio_viewH);<br/>``` |
