## Render Suites

Since we introduced the AEGP API, we've been asked to provide functions for retrieving rendered frames.

These function suites allows you to do just that.

First, specify what you want rendered in the [AEGP_RenderOptionsSuite4](#aegp_renderoptionssuite4) or [AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsSuite1](#aegp_layerrenderoptionssuite1).

Then do the rendering with [AEGP_RenderSuite4](#aegp_rendersuite4).

### AEGP_RenderOptionsSuite4

| **Function**                | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
|-----------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_NewFromItem`          | Returns the `AEGP_RenderOptionsH` associated with a given `AEGP_ItemH`.<br/>If there are no options yet specified, After Effects passes back an `AEGP_RenderOptionsH` with render time set to 0,<br/>time step set to the current frame duration, field render set to `PF_Field_FRAME`, and the depth set to the highest resolution specified within the item.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_NewFromItem(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID        plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_ItemH           itemH,<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  *optionsPH);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_Duplicate`            | Duplicates an `AEGP_RenderOptionsH` into `copyPH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_Duplicate(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID        plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  *copyPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| `AEGP_Dispose`              | Deletes an `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_Dispose(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_SetTime`              | Sets the render time of an `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetTime(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_Time               time);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_GetTime`              | Retrieves the render time of the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetTime(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_Time               *timeP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_SetTimeStep`          | Specifies the time step (duration of a frame) for the referenced `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetTimeStep(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_Time               time_step);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_GetTimeStep`          | Retrieves the time step (duration of a frame) for the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetTimeStep(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_Time               *timePT);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_SetFieldRender`       | Specifies the field settings for the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetFieldRender(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  PF_Field             field_render);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_GetFieldRender`       | Retrieves the field settings for the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetFieldRender(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  PF_Field             *field_renderP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| `AEGP_SetWorldType`         | Specifies the AEGP_WorldType of the output of a given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetWorldType(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_WorldType       type);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_WorldType` will be either `AEGP_WorldType_8` or `AEGP_WorldType_16`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_GetWorldType`         | Retrieves the `AEGP_WorldType` of the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetWorldType(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_WorldType       *typeP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_SetDownsampleFactor`  | Specifies the downsample factor (with independent horizontal and vertical settings) for the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetDownsampleFactor(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_short              x,<br/>  A_short              y);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_GetDownsampleFactor`  | Retrieves the downsample factor for the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetDownsampleFactor(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_short              *xP,<br/>  A_short              *yP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_SetRegionOfInterest`  | Specifies the region of interest sub-rectangle for the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetRegionOfInterest(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  const A_LRect        *roiP)<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_GetRegionOfInterest`  | Retrieves the region of interest sub-rectangle for the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetRegionOfInterest(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_LRect              *roiP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_SetMatteMode`         | Specifies the `AEGP_MatteMode` for the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMatteMode(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_MatteMode       mode);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_MatteMode` will be one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_MatteMode_STRAIGHT`<br/>> - `AEGP_MatteMode_PREMUL_BLACK`<br/>> - `AEGP_MatteMode_PREMUL_BG_COLOR`                                                                                                                                                      |
| `AEGP_GetMatteMode`         | Retrieves the `AEGP_MatteMode` for the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMatteMode(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_MatteMode       *modeP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_GetChannelOrder`      | Gets the `AEGP_ChannelOrder` for the given `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/>`AEGP_ChannelOrder` will be either `AEGP_ChannelOrder_ARGB` or `AEGP_ChannelOrder_BGRA`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetChannelOrder(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_ChannelOrder    *orderP);<br/>```<br/><br/>Factoid: this was added to facilitate live linking with Premiere Pro.                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_SetChannelOrder`      | Sets the `AEGP_ChannelOrder` of the `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetChannelOrder(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_ChannelOrder    order);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_GetRenderGuideLayers` | Passes back a boolean that is true if the render guide layers setting is on.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetRenderGuideLayers)(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_Boolean            *will_renderPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_SetRenderGuideLayers` | Specify whether or not to render guide layers.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetRenderGuideLayers)(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_Boolean            render_themB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_GetRenderQuality`     | Get the render quality of the render queue item.<br/>Quality can be either `AEGP_ItemQuality_DRAFT` or `AEGP_ItemQuality_BEST`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetRenderQuality)(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_ItemQuality     *qualityP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_SetRenderQuality`     | Set the render quality of the render queue item.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetRenderQuality)(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_ItemQuality     quality);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |

### AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsSuite1

!!! note
 New in 13.0

| **Function**                   | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
|--------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_NewFromLayer`            | Returns the `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH` associated with a given `AEGP_LayerH`.<br/>Render time is set to the layer's current time, time step is set to layer's frame duration,<br/>ROI to the layer's nominal bounds, and EffectsToRender to "all".<br/>`optionsPH` must be disposed by calling code.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_NewFromLayer(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID             plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_LayerH               layerH,<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  *optionsPH);<br/>```                                                 |
| `AEGP_NewFromUpstreamOfEffect` | Returns the `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH` from the layer associated with a given `AEGP_EffectRefH`.<br/>Render time is set to the layer's current time, time step is set to layer's frame duration,<br/>ROI to the layer's nominal bounds, and EffectsToRender to the index of `effectH`.<br/>`optionsPH` must be disposed by calling code.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_NewFromUpstreamOfEffect(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID             plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_EffectRefH           effectH,<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  *optionsPH);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_Duplicate`               | Duplicates an `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH` into `copyPH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_Duplicate(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID             plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  *copyPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_Dispose`                 | Deletes an `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_Dispose(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_SetTime`                 | Sets the render time of an `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetTime(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_Time                    time);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_GetTime`                 | Retrieves the render time of the given `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetTime(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_Time                    *timeP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_SetTimeStep`             | Specifies the time step (duration of a frame) for the referenced `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetTimeStep(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_Time                    time_step);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_GetTimeStep`             | Retrieves the time step (duration of a frame) for the given `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetTimeStep(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_Time                    *timePT);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_SetWorldType`            | Specifies the AEGP_WorldType of the output of a given `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetWorldType(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_WorldType            type);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_WorldType` will be either `AEGP_WorldType_8` or `AEGP_WorldType_16`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_GetWorldType`            | Retrieves the AEGP_WorldType of the given `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetWorldType(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_WorldType            *typeP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_SetDownsampleFactor`     | Specifies the downsample factor (with independent horizontal and vertical settings) for the given `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetDownsampleFactor(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_short                   x,<br/>  A_short                   y);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_GetDownsampleFactor`     | Retrieves the downsample factor for the given `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetDownsampleFactor(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  A_short                   *xP,<br/>  A_short                   *yP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_SetMatteMode`            | Specifies the AEGP_MatteMode for the given `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetMatteMode(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_MatteMode            mode);<br/>```<br/><br/>AEGP_MatteMode will be one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_MatteMode_STRAIGHT`<br/>> - `AEGP_MatteMode_PREMUL_BLACK`<br/>> - `AEGP_MatteMode_PREMUL_BG_COLOR`                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_GetMatteMode`            | Retrieves the AEGP_MatteMode for the given `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetMatteMode(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH  optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_MatteMode            *modeP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |

### AEGP_RenderSuite4

| **Function**                        | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
|-------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_RenderAndCheckoutFrame`       | Retrieves an `AEGP_FrameReceiptH` (not the actual pixels) for the frame requested.<br/>Check in this receipt using `AEGP_CheckinFrame` to release memory.<br/><br/>Create the `AEGP_RenderOptionsH` using the [AEGP_RenderOptionsSuite4](#aegp_renderoptionssuite4).<br/><br/>Optionally, the AEGP can pass a function to be called by After Effects if the user cancels the current render,<br/>as well as a refcon (constant reference to opaque data) for use during that function.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_RenderAndCheckoutFrame(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH             optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_RenderSuiteCheckForCancel  cancel_functionP0,<br/>  AEGP_CancelRefcon               cancel_function_refconP0,<br/>  AEGP_FrameReceiptH              *receiptPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| `AEGP_RenderAndCheckoutLayerFrame`  | New in CC 2014. This allows frame checkout of a layer with effects applied at non-render time.<br/>This is useful for an operation that requires the frame, for example, when a button is clicked and it is acceptable to wait for a moment while it is rendering.<br/><br/>Note: Since it is not asynchronous, it will not solve the general problem where custom UI needs to draw based on the frame.<br/><br/>Retrieves an `AEGP_FrameReceiptH` (not the actual pixels) for the layer frame requested.<br/>Check in this receipt using `AEGP_CheckinFrame` to release memory.<br/><br/>Create the `AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH` using `AEGP_NewFromUpstreamOfEffect()`, in [AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsSuite1](#aegp_layerrenderoptionssuite1).<br/><br/>You can actually use `AEGP_NewFromLayer()` to get other layer param's layers with their effects applied.<br/>However, be careful. If you do it in your effect A, and there's an effect B on the other layer that does the same thing during rendering, you'd create an infinite loop.<br/>If you're not doing it for render purposes then it could be okay.<br/><br/>Optionally, the AEGP can pass a function to be called by After Effects if the user cancels the current render,<br/>as well as a refcon (constant reference to opaque data) for use during that function.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_RenderAndCheckoutLayerFrame(<br/>  AEGP_LayerRenderOptionsH        optionsH,<br/>  A_Boolean                       render_plain_layer_frameB,<br/>  AEGP_RenderSuiteCheckForCancel  cancel_functionP0,<br/>  AEGP_CancelRefcon               cancel_function_refconP0,<br/>  AEGP_FrameReceiptH              *receiptPH);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_CheckinFrame`                 | Call this function as soon as your AEGP is done accessing the frame.<br/>After Effects makes caching decisions based on which frames are checked out, so don't hog them!<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_CheckinFrame(<br/>  AEGP_FrameReceiptH  receiptH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_GetReceiptWorld`              | Retrieves the pixels (`AEGP_WorldH`) associated with the referenced `AEGP_FrameReceiptH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetReceiptWorld(<br/>  AEGP_FrameReceiptH  receiptH,<br/>  AEGP_WorldH         *worldPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_GetRenderedRegion`            | Retrieves an `A_LRect` containing the region of the `AEGP_FrameReceiptH's` `AEGP_WorldH` that has already been rendered.<br/>Remember that it's possible for only those portions of an image that have been changed to be rendered,<br/>so it's important to be able to check whether or not that includes the portion you need.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetRenderedRegion(<br/>  AEGP_FrameReceiptH  receiptH,<br/>  A_LRect             *regionP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_IsRenderedFrameSufficient`    | Given two sets of `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`, After Effects will return `TRUE` if the already-rendered pixels are still valid for the proposed `AEGP_RenderOptionsH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_IsRenderedFrameSufficient(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  rendered_optionsH,<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH  proposed_optionsH,<br/>  A_Boolean            *is_sufficientPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_RenderNewItemSoundData`       | Obtains an `AEGP_ItemH's` audio at the given time, of the given duration, in the given format.<br/>The plug-in must dispose of the returned `AEGP_SoundDataH` (which may be NULL if no audio is available).<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_RenderNewItemSoundData(<br/>  AEGP_ItemH                  itemH,<br/>  const A_Time                *start_timePT,<br/>  const A_Time                *durationPT,<br/>  const AEGP_SoundDataFormat  *formatP,<br/>  AEGP_SoundDataH             *new_dataPH);<br/>```<br/><br/>NOTE: This function, if called as part of `AEGP_ItemSuite2`, provides a render interruptible using mouse clicks,<br/>unlike the version published here in `AEGP_RenderSuite`.                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| `AEGP_GetCurrentTimestamp`          | Retrieves the current `AEGP_TimeStamp` of the project.<br/>The `AEGP_TimeStamp` is updated whenever an item is touched in a way that affects rendering.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetCurrentTimestamp(<br/>  AEGP_TimeStamp  *time_stampP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_HasItemChangedSinceTimestamp` | Returns whether the video of an AEGP_ItemH has changed since the given `AEGP_TimeStamp`.<br/><br/>Note: this does not track changes in audio.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_HasItemChangedSinceTimestamp(<br/>  AEGP_ItemH            itemH,<br/>  const A_Time          *start_timeP,<br/>  const A_Time          *durationP,<br/>  const AEGP_TimeStamp  *time_stampP,<br/>  A_Boolean             *changedPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_IsItemWorthwhileToRender`     | Returns whether this frame would be worth rendering externally and checking in to the cache.<br/>A speculative renderer should check this twice: before sending the frame out to render and when it is complete,<br/>before calling `AEGP_NewPlatformWorld()` and checking in.<br/><br/>This function is to be used with `AEGP_HasItemChangedSinceTimestamp()`, not alone.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_IsItemWorthwhileToRender(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH   roH,<br/>  const AEGP_TimeStamp  *time_stampP,<br/>  A_Boolean             *worthwhilePB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_CheckinRenderedFrame`         | Provide a rendered frame (`AEGP_PlatformWorldH`) to After Effects, which adopts it.<br/>`ticksL` is the approximate time required to render the frame.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_CheckinRenderedFrame(<br/>  AEGP_RenderOptionsH    roH,<br/>  const AEGP_TimeStamp*  time_stampP,<br/>  A_u_long               ticksL,<br/>  AEGP_PlatformWorldH    imageH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_GetReceiptGuid`               | New in CS6. Retrieve a GUID for a rendered frame. The memory handle passed back must be disposed.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetReceiptGuid(<br/>  AEGP_FrameReceiptH  receiptH,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle      *guidMH)<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |

## The AEGP_World As We Know It

`AEGP_Worlds` are the common format used throughout the AEGP APIs to describe frames of pixels.

### AEGP_WorldSuite3

| **Function**                         | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
|--------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_New`                           | Returns an allocated, initialized `AEGP_WorldH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_New(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID   plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_WorldType  type,<br/>  A_long          widthL,<br/>  A_long          heightL,<br/>  AEGP_WorldH     *worldPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| `AEGP_Dispose`                       | Disposes of an `AEGP_WorldH`. Use this on every world you allocate.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_Dispose(<br/>  AEGP_WorldH  worldH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_GetType`                       | Returns the type of a given `AEGP_WorldH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetType(<br/>  AEGP_WorldH worldH,<br/>  AEGP_WorldType **typeP);<br/>```<br/><br/>AEGP_WorldType will be one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_WorldType_8`,<br/>> - `AEGP_WorldType_16`,<br/>> - `AEGP_WorldType_32`                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_GetSize`                       | Returns the width and height of the given `AEGP_WorldH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetSize(<br/>  AEGP_WorldH  worldH,<br/>  A_long       *widthPL,<br/>  A_long       *heightPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_GetRowBytes`                   | Returns the rowbytes for the given `AEGP_WorldH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetRowBytes(<br/>  AEGP_WorldH  worldH,<br/>  A_u_long     *row_bytesPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| `AEGP_GetBaseAddr8`                  | Returns the base address of the `AEGP_WorldH` for use in pixel iteration functions.<br/>Will return an error if used on a non-8bpc world.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetBaseAddr8(<br/>  AEGP_WorldH  worldH,<br/>  PF_Pixel8    **base_addrP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| `AEGP_GetBaseAddr16`                 | Returns the base address of the `AEGP_WorldH` for use in pixel iteration functions.<br/>Will return an error if used on a non-16bpc world.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetBaseAddr16(<br/>  AEGP_WorldH  worldH,<br/>  PF_Pixel16   **base_addrP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_GetBaseAddr32`                 | Returns the base address of the `AEGP_WorldH` for use in pixel iteration functions.<br/>Will return an error if used on a non-32bpc world.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetBaseAddr32(<br/>  AEGP_WorldH    worldH,<br/>  PF_PixelFloat  **base_addrP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_FillOutPFEffectWorld`          | Populates and returns a PF_EffectWorld representing the given `AEGP_WorldH`, for use with numerous pixel processing callbacks.<br/><br/>NOTE: This does not give your plug-in ownership of the world referenced; destroy the source `AEGP_WorldH` only if you allocated it.<br/>It just fills out the provided `PF_EffectWorld` to point to the same pixel buffer.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_FillOutPFEffectWorld(<br/>  AEGP_WorldH     worldH,<br/>  PF_EffectWorld  *pf_worldP);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_FastBlur`                      | Performs a fast blur on a given `AEGP_WorldH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_FastBlur(<br/>  A_FpLong      radiusF,<br/>  PF_ModeFlags  mode,<br/>  PF_Quality    quality,<br/>  AEGP_WorldH   worldH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| `AEGP_NewPlatformWorld`              | Creates a new `AEGP_PlatformWorldH` (a pixel world native to the execution platform).<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_NewPlatformWorld(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID        plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_WorldType       type,<br/>  A_long               widthL,<br/>  A_long               heightL,<br/>  AEGP_PlatformWorldH  *worldPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                               |
| `AEGP_DisposePlatformWorld`          | Disposes of an `AEGP_PlatformWorldH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DisposePlatformWorld(<br/>  AEGP_PlatformWorldH  worldH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_NewReferenceFromPlatformWorld` | Retrieves an AEGP_WorldH referring to the given `AEGP_PlatformWorldH`.<br/><br/>NOTE: This doesn't allocate a new world, it simply provides a reference to an existing one.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_NewReferenceFromPlatformWorld(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID        plugin_id,<br/>  AEGP_PlatformWorldH  plat_worldH,<br/>  AEGP_WorldH          *worldPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                            |

---

## Track Mattes and Transform Functions

Use the `AEGP_CompositeSuite` to copy pixel worlds, operate on track mattes, and apply transfer functions.

### AEGP_CompositeSuite2

| **Function**                | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|-----------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_ClearAlphaExceptRect` | For the given `PF_EffectWorld`, sets the alpha to fully transparent except for the specified rectangle.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_ClearAlphaExceptRect(<br/>  A_Rect          *clipped_dst_rectPR,<br/>  PF_EffectWorld  *dstP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_PrepTrackMatte`       | Mattes the pixels in a `PF_EffectWorld` with the `PF_Pixel` described in src_masks, putting the output into an array of pixels dst_mask.<br/><br/>NOTE: Unlike most of the other pixel mangling functions provided by After Effects, this one doesn't take `PF_EffectWorld` arguments;<br/>rather, you can simply pass the data pointer from within the `PF_EffectWorld`.<br/>This can be confusing, but as a bonus, the function pads output appropriately so that `num_pix` pixels are always output.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_PrepTrackMatte(<br/>  A_long          num_pix,<br/>  A_Boolean       deepB,<br/>  const PF_Pixel  *src_mask,<br/>  PF_MaskFlags    mask_flags,<br/>  PF_Pixel        *dst_mask);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_TransferRect`         | Blends two `PF_EffectWorlds` using a transfer mode, with an optional mask.<br/>Pass NULL for the `blend_tablesP0` parameter to perform blending in the current working color space.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_TransferRect(<br/>  PF_Quality               quality,<br/>  PF_ModeFlags             m_flags,<br/>  PF_Field                 field,<br/>  const A_Rect             *src_rec,<br/>  const PF_EffectWorld     *src_world,<br/>  const PF_CompositeMode   *comp_mode,<br/>  PF_EffectBlendingTables  blend_tablesP0,<br/>  const PF_MaskWorld       *mask_world0,<br/>  A_long                   dest_x,<br/>  A_long                   dest_y,<br/>  PF_EffectWorld           *dst_world);<br/>```             |
| `AEGP_CopyBits_LQ`          | Copies a rectangle of pixels (pass a `NULL` rectangle to get all pixels) from one `PF_EffectWorld` to another, at low quality.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_CopyBits_LQ(<br/>  PF_EffectWorld  *src_worldP,<br/>  A_Rect          *src_r,<br/>  A_Rect          *dst_r,<br/>  PF_EffectWorld  *dst_worldP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_CopyBits_HQ_Straight` | Copies a rectangle of pixels (pass a `NULL` rectangle to get all pixels) from one `PF_EffectWorld` to another, at high quality,<br/>with a straight alpha channel.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_CopyBits_HQ_Straight(<br/>  PF_EffectWorld  *src,<br/>  A_Rect          *src_r,<br/>  A_Rect          *dst_r,<br/>  PF_EffectWorld  *dst);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_CopyBits_HQ_Premul`   | Copies a rectangle of pixels (pass a `NULL` rectangle to get all pixels) from one `PF_EffectWorld` to another, at high quality,<br/>premultiplying the alpha channel.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_CopyBits_HQ_Premul(<br/>  PF_EffectWorld  *src,<br/>  A_Rect          *src_r,<br/>  A_Rect          *dst_r,<br/>  PF_EffectWorld  *dst);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |

---

## Work With Audio

`AEGP_SoundDataSuite` allows AEGPs to obtain and manipulate the audio associated with compositions and footage items.

Audio-only items may be added to the render queue using `AEGP_RenderNewItemSoundData()`.

### AEGP_SoundDateSuite1

| **Function**                  | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
|-------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_NewSoundData`           | Creates a new `AEGP_SoundDataH`, of which the plug-in must dispose.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_NewSoundData(<br/>  const AEGP_SoundDataFormat  *formatP,<br/>  AEGP_SoundDataH             *new_dataPH);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_DisposeSoundData`       | Frees an `AEGP_SoundDataH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DisposeSoundData(<br/>  AEGP_SoundDataH  sound_dataH);<br/>```                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_GetSoundDataFormat`     | Obtains information about the format of a given `AEGP_SoundDataH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetSoundDataFormat(<br/>  AEGP_SoundDataH       soundH,<br/>  AEGP_SoundDataFormat  *formatP);<br/>```             |
| `AEGP_LockSoundDataSamples`   | Locks the `AEGP_SoundDataH` in memory.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_LockSoundDataSamples(<br/>  AEGP_SoundDataH  soundH,<br/>  void             **samples);<br/>```                                                |
| `AEGP_UnlockSoundDataSamples` | Unlocks an `AEGP_SoundDataH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_UnlockSoundDataSamples(<br/>  AEGP_SoundDataH  soundH);<br/>```                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_GetNumSamples`          | Obtains the number of samples in the given `AEGP_SoundDataH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNumSamples(<br/>  AEGP_SoundDataH  soundH,<br/>  A_long           *numsamplesPL);<br/>```                            |

---

## Audio Settings

Audio render settings are represented using the `AEGP_SoundDataFormat`.

```default
struct AEGP_SoundDataFormat {
  A_FpLong            sample_rateF;
  AEGP_SoundEncoding  encoding;
  A_long              bytes_per_sampleL;
  A_long              num_channelsL; // 1 for mono, 2 for stereo
} AEGP_SoundDataFormat;
```

`bytes_per_sampleL` is always either `1`, `2`, or `4`, and is ignored if float encoding is specified.

`AEGP_SoundEncoding` is one of the following:

> - `AEGP_SoundEncoding_UNSIGNED_PCM`
> - `AEGP_SoundEncoding_SIGNED_PCM`
> - `AEGP_SoundEncoding_FLOAT`

---

## Render Queue Suite

This suite allows AEGPs to add items the to render queue (using default options), and control the basic state of the render queue.

### AEGP_RenderQueueSuite1

| **Function**                | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
|-----------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_AddCompToRenderQueue` | Adds a composition to the render queue, using default options.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_AddCompToRenderQueue(<br/>  AEGP_CompH     compH,<br/>  const A_char*  pathZ);<br/>```                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_SetRenderQueueState`  | Sets the render queue to one of three valid states.<br/>It is not possible to go from stopped to paused.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetRenderQueueState(<br/>  AEGP_RenderQueueState  state);<br/>```<br/><br/>- `AEGP_RenderQueueState_STOPPED`<br/>- `AEGP_RenderQueueState_PAUSED`<br/>- `AEGP_RenderQueueState_RENDERING` |
| `AEGP_GetRenderQueueState`  | Obtains the current render queue state.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetRenderQueueState(<br/>  AEGP_RenderQueueState  *stateP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                        |

---

## Render Queue Item Suite

Manipulate all aspects of render queue items using this suite.

### AEGP_RQItemSuite4

| **Function**                        | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
|-------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_GetNumRQItems`                | Returns the number of items currently in the render queue.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNumRQItems(<br/>  A_long  *num_itemsPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| `AEGP_GetRQItemByIndex`             | Returns an `AEGP_RQItemRefH` referencing the index'd item.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetRQItemByIndex(<br/>  A_long           rq_item_index,<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  *rq_item_refPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_GetNextRQItem`                | Returns the next `AEGP_RQItemRefH`, for iteration purposes.<br/>To get the first `AEGP_RQItemRefH`, pass `RQ_ITEM_INDEX_NONE` for the `current_rq_itemH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNextRQItem(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  current_rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  *next_rq_itemPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_GetNumOutputModulesForRQItem` | Returns the number of output modules applied to the given `AEGP_RQItemRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNumOutputModulesForRQItem(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  rq_itemH,<br/>  A_long           *num_outmodsPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| `AEGP_GetRenderState`               | Returns TRUE if the `AEGP_RQItemRefH` is set to render (once the user clicks the Render button).<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetRenderState(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  rq_itemH,<br/>  A_Boolean        *will_renderPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_SetRenderState`               | Controls whether or not the `AEGP_RQItemRefH` will render when the user next clicks the Render button.<br/>Returns an error if called during rendering.<br/><br/>This function will return:<br/><br/>- `Err_PARAMETER` if you try to call while `AEGP_RenderQueueState` isn't `AEGP_RenderQueueState_STOPPED`,<br/>- `Err_RANGE` if you pass a status that is illegal in any case, and<br/>- `Err_PARAMETER` if you try to pass a status that doesn't make sense (like trying to queue something for which there's no output path)<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetRenderState(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  rq_itemH,<br/>  A_Boolean        renderB);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_GetStartedTime`               | Returns the time (in seconds, since 1904) that rendering began.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetStartedTime(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  rq_itemH,<br/>  A_Time           *started_timePT);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_GetElapsedTime`               | Returns the time elapsed since rendering began.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetElapsedTime(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  rq_itemH,<br/>  A_Time           *render_timePT);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_GetLogType`                   | Returns the log type for the referenced `AEGP_RQItemRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetLogType(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_LogType     *logtypeP);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_LogtType` will have one of the following values:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_LogType_NONE`<br/>> - `AEGP_LogType_ERRORS_ONLY`<br/>> - `AEGP_LogType_PLUS_SETTINGS`<br/>> - `AEGP_LogType_PER_FRAME_INFO`                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_SetLogType`                   | Specifies the log type to be used with the referenced `AEGP_RQItemRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetLogType(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_LogType     logtype);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| `AEGP_RemoveOutputModule`           | Removes the specified output module from the referenced `AEGP_RQItemRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_RemoveOutputModule(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_GetComment`                   | Updated to support Unicode in `RQItemSuite4`, available in 14.1.<br/>Retrieves the comment associated with the referenced `AEGP_RQItemRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetComment(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle   *unicodeH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_SetComment`                   | Updated to support Unicode in `RQItemSuite4`, available in 14.1.<br/>Specifies the comment associated with the referenced `AEGP_RQItemRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetComment(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH    rq_itemH,<br/>  const A_UTF16Char  *commentZ);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_GetCompFromRQItem`            | Retrieves the `AEGP_CompH` associated with the `AEGP_RQItemRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetCompFromRQItem(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_CompH       *compPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| `AEGP_DeleteRQItem`                 | Deletes the render queue item. Undoable.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_DeleteRQItem(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH  rq_itemH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
