| `AEGP_GetNumJobItemOutputModuleProperties` | Get the number of properties for a job item output module.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNumJobItemOutputModuleProperties(<br/>  AEGP_RQM_SessionId  sessid,<br/>  AEGP_RQM_ItemId     itemid,<br/>  A_long              outputModuleIndex,<br/>  A_long              *num_propertiesPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| `AEGP_GetJobItemOutputModuleProperty`      | Get a specific property off a job item output module.<br/>The property name and values are handle to NULL-terminated A_UTF16Char strings, and must be disposed with `AEGP_FreeMemHandle`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetJobItemOutputModuleProperty(<br/>  AEGP_RQM_SessionId  sessid,<br/>  AEGP_RQM_ItemId     itemid,<br/>  A_long              outputModuleIndex,<br/>  A_long              propertyIndex,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle      *utf_property_namePH0,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle      *utf_property_valuePH0);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_GetJobItemFrameThumbnail`            | Get a buffer with a JPEG-encoded thumbnail of the job item frame.<br/>Pass in the maximum width and height, and the actual dimensions will be passed back.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetJobItemFrameThumbnail(<br/>  AEGP_RQM_SessionId  sessid,<br/>  AEGP_RQM_ItemId     itemid,<br/>  AEGP_RQM_FrameId    frameid,<br/>  A_long              *widthPL,<br/>  A_long              *heightPL,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle      *thumbnailPH0);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |

---

## Output Module Suite

Every item in the render queue has at least one output module specified.

Use this suite to query and control all aspects of the output modules attached to a given render item.

You may also add and remove output modules.

Factoid: For each frame rendered for a given render item, the list of output modules is traversed. So, for frame 0, output module 0, then 1, then 2 are called.

### AEGP_OutputModuleSuite4

| **Function**                    | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
|---------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_GetOutputModuleByIndex`   | Retrieves the indexed output module.<br/><br/>NOTE: `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH` is an opaque data type, and can't be manipulated directly; you must use our accessor functions to modify it.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetOutputModuleByIndex(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  A_long                 outmod_indexL,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  *outmodPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_GetEmbedOptions`          | Retrieves the embedding setting specified for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetEmbedOptions(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_EmbeddingType     *embed_optionsP);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_EmbeddingType` will be one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_Embedding_NOTHING`<br/>> - `AEGP_Embedding_LINK`<br/>> - `AEGP_Embedding_LINK_AND_COPY`                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| `AEGP_SetEmbedOptions`          | Specifies the embedding setting for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetEmbedOptions(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_EmbeddingType     embed_options);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_GetPostRenderAction`      | Retrieves the post-render action setting for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetPostRenderAction(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_PostRenderAction  *actionP);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_PostRenderAction` will be one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_PostRenderOptions_IMPORT`<br/>> - `AEGP_PostRenderOptions_IMPORT_AND_REPLACE_USAGE`<br/>> - `AEGP_PostRenderOptions_SET_PROXY`                                                                                                                                                                |
| `AEGP_SetPostRenderAction`      | Specifies the post-render action setting for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetPostRenderAction(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_PostRenderAction  action);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_GetEnabledOutputs`        | Retrieves which output types are enabled for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetEnabledOutputs(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputTypes       *typesP);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_OutputTypes` will contain one or both of the following values:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_OutputType_VIDEO`<br/>> - `AEGP_OutputType_AUDIO`<br/><br/>NOTE: These are flags, not an enumeration.                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_SetEnabledOutputs`        | Specifies which output types are enabled for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetEnabledOutputs(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputTypes       enabled_types);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| `AEGP_GetOutputChannels`        | Retrieves which video channels are enabled for output in the referenced AEGP_OutputModuleRefH.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetOutputChannels(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_VideoChannels     *outchannelsP);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_VideoChannels` will be one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_VideoChannels_RGB`<br/>> - `AEGP_VideoChannels_RGBA`<br/>> - `AEGP_VideoChannels_ALPHA`                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| `AEGP_SetOutputChannels`        | Specifies which video channels are enabled for output in the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetOutputChannels(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_VideoChannels     outchannels);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_GetStretchInfo`           | Retrieves the stretch information enabled for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`;<br/>whether or not stretching is enabled, whether or not the frame aspect ratio is locked to the composition's, and what quality setting is specified.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetStretchInfo(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  A_Boolean              *enabledPB,<br/>  AEGP_StretchQuality    *qualP,<br/>  A_Boolean              *lockedPB);<br/>```<br/><br/>`AEGP_StretchQuality` will be one of the following:<br/><br/>> - `AEGP_StretchQual_LOW`<br/>> - `AEGP_StretchQual_HIGH`              |
| `AEGP_SetStretchInfo`           | Retrieves the stretch information enabled for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetStretchInfo(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  A_Boolean              is_enabledB,<br/>  AEGP_StretchQuality    quality);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_GetCropInfo`              | Retrieves whether or not the cropping is enabled for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`, and the rectangle to be used.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetCropInfo(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  A_Boolean              *is_enabledBP,<br/>  A_Rect                 *crop_rectP);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_SetCropInfo`              | Specifies whether cropping is enabled for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`, and the rectangle to be used.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetCropInfo(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  A_Boolean              enableB,<br/>  A_Rect                 crop_rect);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| `AEGP_GetSoundFormatInfo`       | Retrieves whether or not audio output is enabled for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`, and the settings to be used.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetSoundFormatInfo(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_SoundDataFormat   *formatP,<br/>  A_Boolean              *enabledPB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_SetSoundFormatInfo`       | Specifies whether or not audio output is enabled for the referenced `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH`, and the settings to be used.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetSoundFormatInfo(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_SoundDataFormat   format_info,<br/>  A_Boolean              enabledB);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| `AEGP_GetOutputFilePath`        | Retrieves the path to which `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH's` output file will be written.<br/>The path is a handle to a NULL-terminated A_UTF16Char string, and must be disposed with `AEGP_FreeMemHandle`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetOutputFilePath(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle         *unicode_pathPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| `AEGP_SetOutputFilePath`        | Specifies the path to which `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH's` output file will be written.<br/>The file path is a NULL-terminated UTF-16 string with platform separators.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetOutputFilePath(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  const A_UTF16Char      *pathZ);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_AddDefaultOutputModule`   | Adds the default output module to the specified `AEGP_RQItemRefH`,<br/>and returns the added output module's `AEGP_OutputModuleRefH` (you wouldn't add it if you didn't plan to mess around with it, would you?).<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_AddDefaultOutputModule(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  *outmodPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| `AEGP_GetExtraOutputModuleInfo` | Retrieves information about the output module.<br/>`format_uniPH` and `info_uniPH` provide the textual description of, and information about, the output module, formatted as the user would see it.<br/>`format_uniPH` and `info_uniPH` will contain NULL-terminated UTF16 strings, of which the caller must dispose.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetExtraOutputModuleInfo(<br/>  AEGP_RQItemRefH        rq_itemH,<br/>  AEGP_OutputModuleRefH  outmodH,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle         *format_uniPH,<br/>  AEGP_MemHandle         *info_uniPH,<br/>  A_Boolean              *is_sequenceBP,<br/>  A_Boolean              *multi_frameBP);<br/>``` |

---

## Working With Effects

These functions provide a way for effects (and AEGPs) to obtain information about the context of an applied effect.

!!! note
 Any time you modify or rely on data from outside the normal render pipeline, you run the risk of dependency problems.

There is no way for After Effects to know that you depend on this external information; consequently, you will not be notified if it changes out from under you.

### AEGP_PFInterfaceSuite1

| **Function**                   | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
|--------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_GetEffectLayer`          | Obtain the layer handle of the layer to which the effect is applied.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetEffectLayer(<br/>  PF_ProgPtr   effect_ref,<br/>  AEGP_LayerH  *layerPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| `AEGP_GetNewEffectForEffect`   | Obtain the `AEGP_EffectRefH` corresponding to the effect.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNewEffectForEffect(<br/>  AEGP_PluginID    aegp_plugin_id,<br/>  PF_ProgPtr       effect_ref,<br/>  AEGP_EffectRefH  *effectPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| `AEGP_ConvertEffectToCompTime` | Retreive the composition time corresponding to the effect's layer time.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_ConvertEffectToCompTime(<br/>  PF_ProgPtr     effect_ref,<br/>  long           what_timeL,<br/>  unsigned long  time_scaleLu,<br/>  A_Time         *comp_timePT);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_GetEffectCamera`         | Obtain the camera (if any) being used by After Effects to view the effect's layer.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetEffectCamera(<br/>  PF_ProgPtr    effect_ref,<br/>  const A_Time  *comp_timePT,<br/>  AEGP_LayerH   camera_layerPH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| `AEGP_GetEffectCameraMatrix`   | Obtain the transform used to move between the layer's coordinate space and that of the containing composition.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetEffectCameraMatrix(<br/>  PF_ProgPtr    effect_ref,<br/>  const A_Time  *comp_timePT,<br/>  A_Matrix4     *camera_matrixP,<br/>  A_FpLong      *dst_to_planePF,<br/>  A_short       *plane_widthPL,<br/>  A_short       *plane_heightPL);<br/>```<br/><br/>NOTE: In cases where the effect's input layer has square pixels, but is in a non-square pixel composition,<br/>you must correct for the pixel aspect ratio by premultiplying the matrix by `(1/parF, 1, 1)`. |

### AEGP_GetEffectCameraMatrix Notes

The model view for the camera matrix is inverse of the matrix obtained from `AEGP_GetEffectCameraMatrix()`.

Also note that our matrix is row-based; OpenGL's is column-based.

---

## Do This Many Times

Utilizes multiple processors (if available) for your computations.

### AEGP_IterateSuite1

| **Function**          | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
|-----------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_GetNumThreads`  | Ask After Effects how many threads are currently available.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_GetNumThreads(<br/>  A_long  *num_threadsPL);<br/>```                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| `AEGP_IterateGeneric` | Specify a function for After Effects to manage on multiple processors.<br/>Can be any function pointer specified by `fn_func`, taking the arguments listed below.<br/>See [Private Data](implementation.md#private-data) for a description of how refconPV is used.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_IterateGeneric(<br/>  A_long  iterationsL,<br/>  void    *refconPV,<br/>  A_Err   (*fn_func)<br/>    (void   *refconPV,<br/>    A_long  thread_indexL,<br/>    A_long  i,<br/>    A_long  iterationsL));<br/>``` |

## File Import Manager Suite

The FIMSuite allows file types handled by AEGPs to appear as part of the After Effects import dialog, and drag-and-drop messaging.

These are not for use by AEIOs! Rather, they are for importing projects which are best represented as After Effects compositions.

### AEGP_FIMSuite3

| **Function**                               | **Purpose**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
|--------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `AEGP_RegisterImportFlavor`                | Registers the name of the file type(s) supported by the plug-in.<br/>Upon return, `imp_refP` will be a valid opaque reference, or `AE_FIM_ImportFlavorRef_NONE`.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_RegisterImportFlavor(<br/>  const char              *nameZ,<br/>  AE_FIM_ImportFlavorRef  *imp_refP);<br/>```                                                                                                    |
| `AEGP_RegisterImportFlavorFileTypes`       | Registers an array of file types and file extensions (the two arrays need not be of equal length) supported by the AEGP.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_RegisterImportFlavorFileTypes(<br/>  AE_FIM_ImportFlavorRef  imp_ref,<br/>  long                    num_filekindsL,<br/>  const AEIO_FileKind     *kindsAP,<br/>  long                    num_fileextsL,<br/>  const AEIO_FileKind     *extsAP);<br/>``` |
| `AEGP_RegisterImportFlavorImportCallbacks` | Register the AEGP functions which will respond to import of different filetypes.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_RegisterImportFlavorImportCallbacks(<br/>  AE_FIM_ImportFlavorRef        ref,<br/>  AE_FIM_ImportFlags            single_flag,<br/>  const AE_FIM_ImportCallbacks  *imp_cbsP);<br/>```                                                                                                           |
| `AEGP_SetImportedItem`                     | Designates an item as having been imported (possibly replacing an existing item), and sets associated import options.<br/><br/>```default<br/>AEGP_SetImportedItem(<br/>  AE_FIM_ImportOptions  imp_options,<br/>  AEGP_ItemH            imported_itemH);<br/>```                                                                                                                                              |
